                       Decorated with authentic furnishings from 1900, this quaint cabin sleeps two and includes access to a laundry room and an exhilarating bathing experience in the Shower House!                       </div>
                      <div data-reactid="2021">
                       This cabin is furnished in the Victorian era with a comfortable full sized bed for two. It shares the Shower House &amp; Laundry with the other cabins and has Wi-Fi provided as well as a small fridge just recently added.
                      </div>

                       We are located on East Lake Tyler, a mere 15 miles from town and 3.2 miles off the highway down a narrow and curvy country lake road. It is away from the hustle and bustle of town with dining and shopping only 20 minutes away. Gas and convenience stores are nearby.
